# Mac to GC Symbol Candidates

## Methodology

- For each named Mac symbol, attempt to match against GC symbols
- **HIGH**: exact name match (after stripping leading underscore)
- **MEDIUM**: same prefix + partial name overlap
- **LOW**: possible but uncertain

## Statistics

- Total GC named symbols: 16738
- Total Mac named symbols: 51134
- Candidate matches found: 6535

- HIGH confidence: 22
- MEDIUM confidence: 6513
- LOW confidence: 0
